	OutputLine(NULL, "……なかなかに意地悪な難易度の爆弾探しゲームでございますわねぇ。」",

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#956f6e>圭一</color>", NULL, "<color=#956f6e>Keiichi</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 1, "ps3/s09/01/170101322", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「沙都子なら見付けられる。",
		   NULL, "\"Você consegue, Satoko.", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 1, "ps3/s09/01/170101323", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "……沙都子に見つけられないなら、俺にも無理だろうな。",
		   NULL, " ...Se você não puder, eu vou poder menos ainda.", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 1, "ps3/s09/01/170101324", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "だから俺は沙都子を信じて、全部を賭けるぜ。」",
		   NULL, " Estou depositando toda minha confiança em você!\"", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	DisableWindow();
	ModDrawCharacter(2, 5, "portrait/ri1_warai_a1_", "0", 160, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 10, 200, TRUE );

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#6972c1>梨花</color>", NULL, "<color=#6972c1>Rika</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 5, "ps3/s09/05/170500243", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「……沙都子なら出来ます。",
		   NULL, "\"......Satoko, você pode fazer isso.", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 5, "ps3/s09/05/170500244", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "………レナを救うためにも、…見つけ出してほしいのです。」",
		   NULL, " É para salvar Rena... encontre-o, por favor.\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DisableWindow();
